name:Z‚Äçh‚Äça‚Äçc‚Äça‚Äçi‚Äçr‚Äço‚Äçu‚Äçs‚Äçi
info:1 King Bed Classic
info:Stayed in June 2024
info:Family
info:7 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted June 2, 2024
msg:The room butler service of InterContinental Hefei is very warm and thoughtful. This time when I stayed at InterContinental Hefei, the hotel butler Xiaoguan contacted me before I checked in and asked me about my specific arrival time and room requirements. It was very considerate. Before we arrived at the hotel, we were upgraded to the executive floor room for free, and we took the initiative to handle late check-out (check-out before 2 pm) and express check-out (when checking out, the room card only needs to be left in the room). The welcome snacks (Anhui specialty Huangshan sesame cakes), fruits, and Thai sparkling water provided by the hotel are all great, and there is also a welcome drink exchange in the lobby coffee bar. However, the Executive Lounge Happy Hour catering service provided by the hotel this time was not enjoyed due to time constraints, which should also be of good quality.
The bed in the superior king-size bed room I stayed in this time was indeed large enough, a 2m*2m bed, and the mattress and bedding were very comfortable, reflecting the quality of InterContinental. The bathroom in the hotel room is also very large. The bathtub with a view is very comfortable for a 1.85-meter-tall person like me to lie in. The rainforest shower head has a comfortable water flow. The toiletries are from the Swiss brand Bairuide, which is exclusive to InterContinental. They are of good quality and have a pleasant aroma. The Internet speed in the room is very fast, the air conditioning is comfortable, and the quality of disposable room supplies is very good. Due to time constraints, I did not go to the hotel's swimming pool and gym this time. I would like to make a suggestion that it would be better to equip a room of this quality with a capsule coffee machine, after all, brewing coffee is not common nowadays.
Finally, I would like to comment on the buffet breakfast of InterContinental Hefei. It is very good, with rich varieties and attentive ingredients. I usually evaluate the quality of a hotel's buffet breakfast based on three points. First, how well the bread is made reflects the level of the hotel's pastry chef; second, whether the beverages and fruits are rich in variety, which reflects the hotel's attentiveness; third, how many types of sausages are there, which reflects the hotel's choice of ingredients. Because these are the varieties of buffet breakfasts in all brand hotels, they are more comparable. The bread of Hefei InterContinental is very soft, and there are rich varieties of drinks and fruits; there are five kinds of sausages, far more than other brand hotels, bacon is divided into soft and hard, and there is Swiss meat bread that I like and is not common. What I praised the most about Hefei InterContinental is the Chinese open counter, which actually has freshly made Guangdong rice rolls, very delicious roujiamo, and very chewy Anhui Taihe flat noodles. In addition, there are all kinds of freshly made Chinese snacks such as pancakes and fried dumplings, with both Chinese, Western, southern and northern flavors, as well as Anhui regional cuisine. The hotel buffet restaurant is very attentive.

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:1King 1 Bedroom Suite LoungeAccess SwanLake View
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Family
info:22 Reviews
rating:4.6
posted:Posted May 11, 2024
msg:In order to avoid the large number of tourists during the May Day holiday, I chose a less popular city - Hefei. Unexpectedly, the electronic music festival held by Xiao Yangge made Hefei's May Day holiday this year also very popular.
Before coming here, I had been hesitating between the InterContinental and Grand Hyatt hotels. However, since the reservation of the Grand Hyatt hotel could not be cancelled, I finally chose the InterContinental, after all, in case the plan changed.
Facts have proved that my choice was right.
First of all, the hotel is conveniently located.
The hotel is located on the shore of the beautiful Swan Lake. The water of Swan Lake is clear, and the banks are shaded by trees, birds are singing, and flowers are fragrant. Walking by the lake is refreshing. Standing in front of the floor-to-ceiling window of the hotel room and looking into the distance, the beautiful scenery of Swan Lake is unobstructed. On the left side of the lake is the Anhui Radio and Television Center, which has a unique shape and the outer wall is full of characters in seal script; on the right is the Hefei Grand Theater, which looks like layers of waves from a distance. There are also large shopping malls near the hotel, such as Mixc, Yintai, etc., with a full range of food, drink and entertainment.
Second, the service is meticulous and thoughtful.
1. The concierge at the hotel entrance was elegant and well-dressed. They opened the car door and took the luggage for the guests, and greeted the guests respectfully. What surprised me even more was that the hotel also helped the guests deliver takeaways to the room, which was not available in the five-star hotels I had stayed in before. It deserves praise! However, since the hotel was full during the May Day holiday, their workload was undoubtedly increased. They were really hard!
2. The front desk staff warmly received us. In order to facilitate our choice, they also asked colleagues to take us to see the room type, which made me very satisfied. Although I didn‚Äôt stay in the floor and orientation I wanted, their attitude still calmed me down a lot. In addition, our return flight was late, and I thanked Xiao Zhao from the reservation depar**ent for helping me delay check-out until 4 pm.
3. The room service was responsive and fast. The room was clean, but it would be better if it could be more meticulous.
Third, the rich diet was impressive.
1. The happy hour in the executive lounge should be the most abundant and sincere of all the hotels I have stayed in. It is a small buffet with Chinese and Western food, and even Peking duck sliced ‚Äã‚Äãon site. Although there were too many people and the service staff were too busy, resulting in no plates, it is understandable. After all, there are not many guests staying here on weekdays, and the service staff lacks experience in dealing with it.
2. The breakfast in the Western restaurant on the first floor is also not perfunctory. There are rich and varied varieties, especially Chinese dishes, which are full of local Anhui characteristics. From Anhui Satang, Huainan beef soup to Taihe flat noodles, there is everything, as well as pan-fried buns, chive boxes, fried dumplings... All kinds of pasta are dazzling, and there are also Cantonese steamed points and rice rolls. Friends who like Chinese cuisine must not miss it. However, if you think that only the pasta here is delicious, you think too much. Bread and cake are also delicious, especially the rock-roasted croissant, which has a crispy skin and full of cheese inside, and has a rich taste.
After praising so much, I also want to complain.
What I am not satisfied with is the layout of the room. The living room is too small, the coffee table in the middle is short and small, and the round table in the corner should be a desk, which feels very crowded. The cloakroom is relatively small, and there is not enough space to hang clothes. Another biggest problem is that the suite has only one bathroom, which I don‚Äôt think I have encountered in the InterContinental Hotels I have stayed in before. However, the shower room is quite large and faces Swan Lake.
In short, I am very satisfied with my stay at InterContinental Hefei this time, and I hope to continue to work hard and reach a higher level!
